<script type="text/html" id="template__video-modal">
<div class="embed-responsive embed-responsive-%%ratio%%">
	<iframe class="embed-responsive-item" src="%%url%%" frameborder="0" allow="accelerometer; autoplay; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture" allowfullscreen></iframe>

<script>
(function($) {
	$(function() {

		$('#videoModal').on('show.bs.modal', function(event) {
			setTimeout(() => {
				$('.modal-backdrop').addClass('_darker');
				
			}, 100);
			
			let $rel = $(event.relatedTarget);
			let template = $('#template__video-modal').text();
			template = template.replace('%%ratio%%', $rel.data('ratio') 
				? $rel.data('ratio').replace(/:/, 'by') : '16by9'
			);
			template = template.replace('%%url%%', $rel.data('videoSrc'));
			template = $(template);
			$('#videoEmbed').empty().append(template);
			
		}).on('hidden.bs.modal', function(event) {
			$('#videoEmbed').empty();
		});
	});
})(jQuery);
